\doxysubsection{详细描述}
\subsubsection*{template$<$class RCU, class Ordered\+List, class Traits$>$\newline
class cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Michael\+Hash\+Set$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Ordered\+List, Traits $>$}
Michael\textquotesingle{}s hash set, \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1urcu_cds_urcu_desc}{RCU} specialization 

\label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_MichaelHashSet_rcu}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_MichaelHashSet_rcu}%
 Source\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \mbox{[}2002\mbox{]} Maged Michael "{}\+High performance dynamic lock-\/free hash tables and list-\/based sets"{}
\end{DoxyItemize}

Michael\textquotesingle{}s hash table algorithm is based on lock-\/free ordered list and it is very simple. The main structure is an array {\ttfamily T} of size {\ttfamily M}. Each element in {\ttfamily T} is basically a pointer to a hash bucket, implemented as a singly linked list. The array of buckets cannot be dynamically expanded. However, each bucket may contain unbounded number of items.

Template parameters are\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily RCU} -\/ one of \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1urcu_cds_urcu_gc}{RCU type}
\item {\ttfamily Ordered\+List} -\/ ordered list implementation used as bucket for hash set, for example, \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{Michael\+List}, \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{Lazy\+List}. The intrusive ordered list implementation specifies the type {\ttfamily T} stored in the hash-\/set, the reclamation schema {\ttfamily GC} used by hash-\/set, the comparison functor for the type {\ttfamily T} and other features specific for the ordered list.
\item {\ttfamily Traits} -\/ type traits, default is {\ttfamily \doxylink{structcds_1_1intrusive_1_1michael__set_1_1traits}{michael\+\_\+set\+::traits}}. Instead of defining {\ttfamily Traits} struct you can use option-\/based syntax with {\ttfamily \doxylink{structcds_1_1intrusive_1_1michael__set_1_1make__traits}{michael\+\_\+set\+::make\+\_\+traits}} metafunction.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Usage}
Before including {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\doxylink{intrusive_2michael__set__rcu_8h}{cds/intrusive/michael\+\_\+set\+\_\+rcu.\+h}\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}} you should include appropriate RCU header file, see \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1urcu_cds_urcu_gc}{RCU type} for list of existing RCU class and corresponding header files. For example, for \doxylink{classcds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01general__buffered_3_01_buffer_00_01_lock_00_01_backoff_01_4_01_4_cds_urcu_general_buffered_gc}{general-\/purpose buffered RCU} you should include\+:

typedef michael\+\_\+set\+::details\+::iterator$<$ internal\+\_\+bucket\+\_\+type, \mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a65e9886d74aaee76545e83dd09011727}{false}} $>$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Michael\+Hash\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Ordered\+List, Traits $>$\+::iterator}



Forward iterator 

The forward iterator for Michael\textquotesingle{}s set is based on {\ttfamily Ordered\+List} forward iterator and has some features\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item it has no post-\/increment operator
\item it iterates items in unordered fashion
\item The iterator cannot be moved across thread boundary because it may contain GC\textquotesingle{}s guard that is thread-\/private GC data.
\end{DoxyItemize}

Iterator thread safety depends on type of {\ttfamily Ordered\+List\+:} 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item for {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{Michael\+List}} and {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{Lazy\+List}\+:} iterator guarantees safety even if you delete the item that iterator points to because that item is guarded by hazard pointer. However, in case of concurrent deleting operations it is no guarantee that you iterate all item in the set. Moreover, a crash is possible when you try to iterate the next element that has been deleted by concurrent thread. Use this iterator on the concurrent container for debugging purpose only.
\item for {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_iterable_list}{Iterable\+List}\+:} iterator is thread-\/safe. You may use it freely in concurrent environment. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_a7796e2c820662e07a59122b498a97167}\index{cds::intrusive::MichaelHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, OrderedList, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::MichaelHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, OrderedList, Traits $>$}!iterator@{iterator}}
\index{iterator@{iterator}!cds::intrusive::MichaelHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, OrderedList, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::MichaelHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, OrderedList, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{iterator}{iterator}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_a7796e2c820662e07a59122b498a97167} 
template$<$class RCU, class Ordered\+List, class Traits$>$ \\
typedef michael\+\_\+set\+::details\+::iterator$<$ internal\+\_\+bucket\+\_\+type, \mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a65e9886d74aaee76545e83dd09011727}{false}} $>$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Michael\+Hash\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Ordered\+List, Traits $>$\+::iterator}



Forward iterator 

The forward iterator for Michael\textquotesingle{}s set is based on {\ttfamily Ordered\+List} forward iterator and has some features\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item it has no post-\/increment operator
\item it iterates items in unordered fashion
\end{DoxyItemize}

You may safely use iterators in multi-\/threaded environment only under RCU lock. Otherwise, a crash is possible if another thread deletes the element the iterator points to.

\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Michael\+Hash\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Ordered\+List, Traits $>$\+::\+Michael\+Hash\+Set (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{n\+Max\+Item\+Count}{, }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{n\+Load\+Factor}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Initialize hash set 

The Michael\textquotesingle{}s hash set is an unbounded container, but its hash table is non-\/expandable. At construction time you should pass estimated maximum item count and a load factor. The load factor is average size of one bucket -\/ a small number between 1 and 10. The bucket is an ordered single-\/linked list, the complexity of searching in the bucket is linear {\ttfamily O(n\+Load\+Factor)}. The constructor defines hash table size as rounding {\ttfamily n\+Max\+Item\+Count / n\+Load\+Factor} up to nearest power of two. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em n\+Max\+Item\+Count} & estimation of max item count in the hash set  \\
\hline
{\em n\+Load\+Factor} & load factor\+: average size of the bucket \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Michael\+Hash\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Ordered\+List, Traits $>$\+::\+Michael\+Hash\+Set (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{n\+Max\+Item\+Count}{, }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{n\+Load\+Factor}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Initializes hash set 

The Michael\textquotesingle{}s hash set is an unbounded container, but its hash table is non-\/expandable. At construction time you should pass estimated maximum item count and a load factor. The load factor is average size of one bucket -\/ a small number between 1 and 10. The bucket is an ordered single-\/linked list, searching in the bucket has linear complexity {\ttfamily O(n\+Load\+Factor)}. The constructor defines hash table size as rounding {\ttfamily n\+Max\+Item\+Count / n\+Load\+Factor} up to nearest power of two. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em n\+Max\+Item\+Count} & estimation of max item count in the hash set  \\
\hline
{\em n\+Load\+Factor} & load factor\+: estimation of max number of items in the bucket. Small integer up to 10. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\index{clear@{clear}!cds::intrusive::MichaelHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, OrderedList, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::MichaelHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, OrderedList, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{clear()}{clear()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_afc443797d75f7976c82b84452cc5a610} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Michael\+Hash\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Ordered\+List, Traits $>$\+::clear (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Clears the set (non-\/atomic) 

The function unlink all items from the set. The function is not atomic. It cleans up each bucket and then resets the item counter to zero. If there are a thread that performs insertion while {\ttfamily clear}() is working the result is undefined in general case\+: {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_ae73d85a515d783c045cc8bc33a0f6a63}{empty()}} may return {\ttfamily true} but the set may contain item(s). Therefore, {\ttfamily clear}() may be used only for debugging purposes.

For each item the {\ttfamily disposer} is called after unlinking. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_a4073a895f77897f819b649185b33825e}\index{cds::intrusive::MichaelHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, OrderedList, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::MichaelHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, OrderedList, Traits $>$}!clear@{clear}}
\index{clear@{clear}!cds::intrusive::MichaelHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, OrderedList, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::MichaelHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, OrderedList, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{clear()}{clear()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}

template$<$class RCU, class Ordered\+List, class Traits$>$ \\

Clears the set (non-\/atomic) 

The function unlink all items from the set. The function is not atomic. It cleans up each bucket and then resets the item counter to zero. If there are a thread that performs insertion while {\ttfamily clear} is working the result is undefined in general case\+: {\ttfamily  \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_ae73d85a515d783c045cc8bc33a0f6a63}{empty()} } may return {\ttfamily true} but the set may contain item(s). Therefore, {\ttfamily clear} may be used only for debugging purposes.

For each item the {\ttfamily disposer} is called after unlinking. 函数调用图\+:

\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Michael\+Hash\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Ordered\+List, Traits $>$\+::contains (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{key}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Checks whether the set contains {\ttfamily key} 

The function searches the item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} and returns {\ttfamily true} if the key is found, and {\ttfamily false} otherwise.

Note the hash functor specified for class {\ttfamily Traits} template parameter should accept a parameter of type {\ttfamily Q} that can be not the same as {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_a5d3f41494e647ab88a7301dae2cec6a0}{value\+\_\+type}}. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_a5647c035aaa2aedb4aec90b6a81f0bad}\index{cds::intrusive::MichaelHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, OrderedList, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::MichaelHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, OrderedList, Traits $>$}!contains@{contains}}

\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Michael\+Hash\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Ordered\+List, Traits $>$\+::contains (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{key}{, }\item[{Less}]{pred}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Checks whether the set contains {\ttfamily key} using {\ttfamily pred} predicate for searching 

The function is an analog of {\ttfamily contains( key )} but {\ttfamily pred} is used for key comparing. {\ttfamily Less} functor has the interface like {\ttfamily std\+::less}. {\ttfamily Less} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the set. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_a21387057a851f8724125b46ae8532b17}\index{cds::intrusive::MichaelHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, OrderedList, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::MichaelHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, OrderedList, Traits $>$}!contains@{contains}}

The function is an analog of {\ttfamily contains( key )} but {\ttfamily pred} is used for key comparing. {\ttfamily Less} functor has the interface like {\ttfamily std\+::less}. {\ttfamily Less} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the set. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_a98a7de3b2636bbb8ce78f81c769cdbbe}\index{cds::intrusive::MichaelHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, OrderedList, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::MichaelHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, OrderedList, Traits $>$}!empty@{empty}}

\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_MichaelHashSet_rcu_erase_func}%
The function searches an item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} in the set, call {\ttfamily f} functor with item found, and unlinks it from the set. The \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_a66dc113c2b6d9311ceaa332b48de4c40}{disposer} specified in {\ttfamily Ordered\+List} class template parameter is called by garbage collector {\ttfamily GC} asynchronously.

The {\ttfamily Func} interface is 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}

\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{erase\_at()}{erase\_at()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_a45607404282eeab10b20e3d22889b2a3} 
std\+::enable\+\_\+if$<$ std\+::is\+\_\+same$<$ Iterator, \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_a7796e2c820662e07a59122b498a97167}{iterator}} $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__impl__opengl3__loader_8h_abe8e049f756b5ba547bda825af81b645}{\+::value}} \&\&is\+\_\+iterable\+\_\+list$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_a2c7586c2c778c2fd5562adbd21fde73b}{ordered\+\_\+list}} $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__impl__opengl3__loader_8h_abe8e049f756b5ba547bda825af81b645}{\+::value}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__impl__opengl3__loader_8h_ae8396ff85d63082521e3324820df1009}{\+::type}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Michael\+Hash\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Ordered\+List, Traits $>$\+::erase\+\_\+at (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Iterator const \&}]{iter}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Deletes the item pointed by iterator {\ttfamily iter} (only for {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_iterable_list}{Iterable\+List}} based set) 

Returns {\ttfamily true} if the operation is successful, {\ttfamily false} otherwise. The function can return {\ttfamily false} if the node the iterator points to has already been deleted by other thread.

The function does not invalidate the iterator, it remains valid and can be used for further traversing.

\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
{\ttfamily erase\+\_\+at}() is supported only for {\ttfamily Michael\+Hash\+Set} based on {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_iterable_list}{Iterable\+List}}. 
\end{DoxyNote}

\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Michael\+Hash\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Ordered\+List, Traits $>$\+::erase\+\_\+with (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} \&}]{key}{, }\item[{Less}]{pred}{, }\item[{Func}]{f}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Deletes the item from the set using {\ttfamily pred} predicate for searching 

The function is an analog of \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_MichaelHashSet_rcu_erase_func}{erase(Q const\&)} but {\ttfamily pred} is used for key comparing. {\ttfamily Less} functor has the interface like {\ttfamily std\+::less}. {\ttfamily pred} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the set. 函数调用图\+:

Deletes the item from the set using {\ttfamily pred} predicate for searching 

The function is an analog of \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_cds_intrusive_MichaelHashSet_hp_erase}{erase(Q const\&)} but {\ttfamily pred} is used for key comparing. {\ttfamily Less} functor has the interface like {\ttfamily std\+::less}. {\ttfamily pred} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the set. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_a4f7e3cfb8c5a960eeab1b0c5d8b3cd25}\index{cds::intrusive::MichaelHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, OrderedList, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::MichaelHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, OrderedList, Traits $>$}!erase\_with@{erase\_with}}

Deletes the item from the set using {\ttfamily pred} predicate for searching 

The function is an analog of \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_cds_intrusive_MichaelHashSet_hp_erase_func}{erase(Q const\&, Func)} but {\ttfamily pred} is used for key comparing. {\ttfamily Less} functor has the interface like {\ttfamily std\+::less}. {\ttfamily pred} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the set. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_ab08375606cbee10baee357b071f4cd52}\index{cds::intrusive::MichaelHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, OrderedList, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::MichaelHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, OrderedList, Traits $>$}!extract@{extract}}
\index{extract@{extract}!cds::intrusive::MichaelHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, OrderedList, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::MichaelHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, OrderedList, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{extract()}{extract()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_ab08375606cbee10baee357b071f4cd52} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_a2279c00d35cf91d395f317316ca76678}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Michael\+Hash\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Ordered\+List, Traits $>$\+::extract (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{key}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Extracts the item with specified {\ttfamily key} 

\label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_cds_intrusive_MichaelHashSet_hp_extract}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_cds_intrusive_MichaelHashSet_hp_extract}%
The function searches an item with key equal to {\ttfamily key}, unlinks it from the set, and returns an guarded pointer to the item extracted. If {\ttfamily key} is not found the function returns an empty guarded pointer.

Note the compare functor should accept a parameter of type {\ttfamily Q} that may be not the same as {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_a5d3f41494e647ab88a7301dae2cec6a0}{value\+\_\+type}}.

The {\ttfamily disposer} specified in {\ttfamily Ordered\+List} class\textquotesingle{} template parameter is called automatically by garbage collector {\ttfamily GC} when returned \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_a2279c00d35cf91d395f317316ca76678}{guarded\+\_\+ptr} object will be destroyed or released. \begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Each {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_a2279c00d35cf91d395f317316ca76678}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} object uses the GC\textquotesingle{}s guard that can be limited resource.
\end{DoxyNote}

\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_a37067daedc53a0b43b03041dd79be4a1}{exempt\+\_\+ptr}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Michael\+Hash\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Ordered\+List, Traits $>$\+::extract (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{key}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Extracts an item from the set 

\label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_MichaelHashSet_rcu_extract}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_MichaelHashSet_rcu_extract}%
The function searches an item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} in the set, unlinks it from the set, and returns \doxylink{classcds_1_1urcu_1_1exempt__ptr}{exempt\+\_\+ptr} pointer to the item found. If the item with the key equal to {\ttfamily key} is not found the function returns an empty {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_a37067daedc53a0b43b03041dd79be4a1}{exempt\+\_\+ptr}}.

\doxylink{struct_depends}{Depends} on {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_a2c7586c2c778c2fd5562adbd21fde73b}{ordered\+\_\+list}} you should or should not lock RCU before calling of this function\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item for the set based on \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_MichaelList_rcu}{Michael\+List} RCU should not be locked
\item for the set based on \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_LazyList_rcu}{Lazy\+List} RCU should be locked
\end{DoxyItemize}

See ordered list implementation for details.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_a1e36fd52d7d427979475c072552717d2} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_a2279c00d35cf91d395f317316ca76678}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Michael\+Hash\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Ordered\+List, Traits $>$\+::extract\+\_\+with (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{key}{, }\item[{Less}]{pred}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Extracts the item using compare functor {\ttfamily pred} 

The function is an analog of \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_cds_intrusive_MichaelHashSet_hp_extract}{extract(Q const\&)} but {\ttfamily pred} predicate is used for key comparing.

{\ttfamily Less} functor has the semantics like {\ttfamily std\+::less} but should take arguments of type \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_a5d3f41494e647ab88a7301dae2cec6a0}{value\+\_\+type} and {\ttfamily Q} in any order. {\ttfamily pred} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the list. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_abdd5210cc3931c4c19b76d4f023d5186}\index{cds::intrusive::MichaelHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, OrderedList, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::MichaelHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, OrderedList, Traits $>$}!extract\_with@{extract\_with}}
\index{extract\_with@{extract\_with}!cds::intrusive::MichaelHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, OrderedList, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::MichaelHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, OrderedList, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{extract\_with()}{extract\_with()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_abdd5210cc3931c4c19b76d4f023d5186} 
template$<$class RCU, class Ordered\+List, class Traits$>$ \\
template$<$typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}}, typename Less$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_a37067daedc53a0b43b03041dd79be4a1}{exempt\+\_\+ptr}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Michael\+Hash\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Ordered\+List, Traits $>$\+::extract\+\_\+with (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{key}{, }\item[{Less}]{pred}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Extracts an item from the set using {\ttfamily pred} predicate for searching 

The function is an analog of {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_a4e26310eb2e893c314f6d561fe5ed0ec}{extract(\+Q const\&)}} but {\ttfamily pred} is used for key comparing. {\ttfamily Less} functor has the interface like {\ttfamily std\+::less}. {\ttfamily pred} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the set. 函数调用图\+:

Finds {\ttfamily key} and returns iterator pointed to the item found (only for {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_iterable_list}{Iterable\+List}})

\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Michael\+Hash\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Ordered\+List, Traits $>$\+::find (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} \&}]{key}{, }\item[{Func}]{f}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Finds the key {\ttfamily key} 

\label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_cds_intrusive_MichaelHashSet_hp_find_func}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_cds_intrusive_MichaelHashSet_hp_find_func}%
The function searches the item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} and calls the functor {\ttfamily f} for item found. The interface of {\ttfamily Func} functor is\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set}{functor}}\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set}{operator()}}(\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set}{item}},\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set}{Q}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set}{key}}\ );}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}
 where {\ttfamily item} is the item found, {\ttfamily key} is the {\ttfamily find} function argument.

The functor may change non-\/key fields of {\ttfamily item}. Note that the functor is only guarantee that {\ttfamily item} cannot be disposed during functor is executing. The functor does not serialize simultaneous access to the set {\ttfamily item}. If such access is possible you must provide your own synchronization schema on item level to exclude unsafe item modifications.

The {\ttfamily key} argument is non-\/const since it can be used as {\ttfamily f} functor destination i.\+e., the functor may modify both arguments.

Note the hash functor specified for class {\ttfamily Traits} template parameter should accept a parameter of type {\ttfamily Q} that can be not the same as {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_a5d3f41494e647ab88a7301dae2cec6a0}{value\+\_\+type}}.

The function returns {\ttfamily true} if {\ttfamily key} is found, {\ttfamily false} otherwise. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_ae0e21e536823b99bd217a9b842821a37}\index{cds::intrusive::MichaelHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, OrderedList, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::MichaelHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, OrderedList, Traits $>$}!find@{find}}
\index{find@{find}!cds::intrusive::MichaelHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, OrderedList, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::MichaelHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, OrderedList, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{find()}{find()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [3/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_ae0e21e536823b99bd217a9b842821a37} 
template$<$class RCU, class Ordered\+List, class Traits$>$ \\

\doxylink{struct_find}{Find} the key {\ttfamily key} 

\label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_MichaelHashSet_rcu_find_func}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_MichaelHashSet_rcu_find_func}%
The function searches the item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} and calls the functor {\ttfamily f} for item found. The interface of {\ttfamily Func} functor is\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set}{functor}}\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set}{operator()}}(\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set}{item}},\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set}{Q}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set}{key}}\ );}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}
 where {\ttfamily item} is the item found, {\ttfamily key} is the {\ttfamily find} function argument.

The functor can change non-\/key fields of {\ttfamily item}. The functor does not serialize simultaneous access to the set {\ttfamily item}. If such access is possible you must provide your own synchronization schema on item level to exclude unsafe item modifications.

The {\ttfamily key} argument is non-\/const since it can be used as {\ttfamily f} functor destination i.\+e., the functor can modify both arguments.

Note the hash functor specified for class {\ttfamily Traits} template parameter should accept a parameter of type {\ttfamily Q} that can be not the same as {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_a5d3f41494e647ab88a7301dae2cec6a0}{value\+\_\+type}}.

The function returns {\ttfamily true} if {\ttfamily key} is found, {\ttfamily false} otherwise. 函数调用图\+:

std\+::enable\+\_\+if$<$ std\+::is\+\_\+same$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__impl__opengl3__loader_8h_abe8e049f756b5ba547bda825af81b645}{\+::value}} \&\&is\+\_\+iterable\+\_\+list$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_a2c7586c2c778c2fd5562adbd21fde73b}{ordered\+\_\+list}} $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__impl__opengl3__loader_8h_abe8e049f756b5ba547bda825af81b645}{\+::value}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_a7796e2c820662e07a59122b498a97167}{iterator}} $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__impl__opengl3__loader_8h_ae8396ff85d63082521e3324820df1009}{\+::type}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Michael\+Hash\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Ordered\+List, Traits $>$\+::find\+\_\+with (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} \&}]{key}{, }\item[{Less}]{pred}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Finds {\ttfamily key} using {\ttfamily pred} predicate and returns iterator pointed to the item found (only for {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_iterable_list}{Iterable\+List}}) 

The function is an analog of {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_afaaa5f30c98a04ddc5a18b53b862b465}{find(\+Q\&)}} but {\ttfamily pred} is used for key comparing. {\ttfamily Less} functor has the interface like {\ttfamily std\+::less}. {\ttfamily pred} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the set.

If {\ttfamily key} is not found the function returns {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_a52980decfb68edb1be7c4bf9393ad179}{end()}}.

\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
This function is supported only for the set based on {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_iterable_list}{Iterable\+List}} 
\end{DoxyNote}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_a10ba92bcc0e0d47508ee713d8196704d} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_a2279c00d35cf91d395f317316ca76678}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Michael\+Hash\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Ordered\+List, Traits $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{structget}{\+::get}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{key}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Finds the key {\ttfamily key} and return the item found 

\label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_cds_intrusive_MichaelHashSet_hp_get}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_cds_intrusive_MichaelHashSet_hp_get}%
The function searches the item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} and returns the guarded pointer to the item found. If {\ttfamily key} is not found the function returns an empty {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_a2279c00d35cf91d395f317316ca76678}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}}.

\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Each {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_a2279c00d35cf91d395f317316ca76678}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} object uses one GC\textquotesingle{}s guard which can be limited resource.
\end{DoxyNote}

Note the compare functor specified for {\ttfamily Ordered\+List} template parameter should accept a parameter of type {\ttfamily Q} that can be not the same as {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_a5d3f41494e647ab88a7301dae2cec6a0}{value\+\_\+type}}. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_a7d4d510fa9ee5e3da0710837e1ad9c83}\index{cds::intrusive::MichaelHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, OrderedList, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::MichaelHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, OrderedList, Traits $>$}!get@{get}}

template$<$class RCU, class Ordered\+List, class Traits$>$ \\

\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_a2d1f8f7bebac9802b06c85a5b2bfeaf8}{raw\+\_\+ptr}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Michael\+Hash\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Ordered\+List, Traits $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{structget}{\+::get}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{key}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Finds the key {\ttfamily key} and return the item found 

\label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_MichaelHashSet_rcu_get}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_MichaelHashSet_rcu_get}%
The function searches the item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} and returns the pointer to item found. If {\ttfamily key} is not found it returns {\ttfamily nullptr}. Note the type of returned value depends on underlying {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_a2c7586c2c778c2fd5562adbd21fde73b}{ordered\+\_\+list}}. For details, see documentation of ordered list you use.

Note the compare functor should accept a parameter of type {\ttfamily Q} that can be not the same as {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_a5d3f41494e647ab88a7301dae2cec6a0}{value\+\_\+type}}.

RCU should be locked before call of this function. Returned item is valid only while RCU is locked\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_a87382d00ea366b80c08e0659db9d2972} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_a2279c00d35cf91d395f317316ca76678}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Michael\+Hash\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Ordered\+List, Traits $>$\+::get\+\_\+with (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{key}{, }\item[{Less}]{pred}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Finds the key {\ttfamily key} and return the item found 

The function is an analog of \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_cds_intrusive_MichaelHashSet_hp_get}{get( Q const\&)} but {\ttfamily pred} is used for comparing the keys.

{\ttfamily Less} functor has the semantics like {\ttfamily std\+::less} but should take arguments of type \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_a5d3f41494e647ab88a7301dae2cec6a0}{value\+\_\+type} and {\ttfamily Q} in any order. {\ttfamily pred} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the set. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_a9b416f17c4623896b662262bf2adddbb}\index{cds::intrusive::MichaelHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, OrderedList, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::MichaelHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, OrderedList, Traits $>$}!get\_with@{get\_with}}
\index{get\_with@{get\_with}!cds::intrusive::MichaelHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, OrderedList, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::MichaelHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, OrderedList, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{get\_with()}{get\_with()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_a9b416f17c4623896b662262bf2adddbb} 
template$<$class RCU, class Ordered\+List, class Traits$>$ \\
template$<$typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}}, typename Less$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_a2d1f8f7bebac9802b06c85a5b2bfeaf8}{raw\+\_\+ptr}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Michael\+Hash\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Ordered\+List, Traits $>$\+::get\+\_\+with (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{key}{, }\item[{Less}]{pred}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Finds the key {\ttfamily key} and return the item found 

The function is an analog of \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_MichaelHashSet_rcu_get}{get(Q const\&)} but {\ttfamily pred} is used for comparing the keys.

{\ttfamily Less} functor has the semantics like {\ttfamily std\+::less} but should take arguments of type \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_a5d3f41494e647ab88a7301dae2cec6a0}{value\+\_\+type} and {\ttfamily Q} in any order. {\ttfamily pred} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the set. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_ace6c55a2a940f8992362eeb51f402dcf}\index{cds::intrusive::MichaelHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, OrderedList, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::MichaelHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, OrderedList, Traits $>$}!insert@{insert}}

Inserts new node 

The function inserts {\ttfamily val} in the set if it does not contain an item with key equal to {\ttfamily val}.

Returns {\ttfamily true} if {\ttfamily val} is placed into the set, {\ttfamily false} otherwise. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_a30ccca2ed2f15c2e85d54beb0694839c}\index{cds::intrusive::MichaelHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, OrderedList, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::MichaelHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, OrderedList, Traits $>$}!insert@{insert}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{insert()}{insert()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [3/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_a2d7b1098f54ad30030317c8c52d46ac6} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Michael\+Hash\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Ordered\+List, Traits $>$\+::insert (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_a5d3f41494e647ab88a7301dae2cec6a0}{value\+\_\+type}} \&}]{val}{, }\item[{Func}]{f}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Inserts new node 

This function is intended for derived non-\/intrusive containers.

The function allows to split creating of new item into two part\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item create item with key only
\item insert new item into the set
\item if inserting is success, calls {\ttfamily f} functor to initialize value-\/field of {\ttfamily val}.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The functor signature is\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{benchmarks_2async__task_2async__task_8hpp_abce53bb5cc1ee70cdc013fd9b93547eb}{func}}(\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_a5d3f41494e647ab88a7301dae2cec6a0}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set}{val}}\ );}

\end{DoxyCode}
 where {\ttfamily val} is the item inserted.

The user-\/defined functor is called only if the inserting is success.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
For \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_cds_intrusive_MichaelList_hp}{Michael\+List} as the bucket see \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1intrusive_cds_intrusive_item_creating}{insert item troubleshooting}. \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_cds_intrusive_LazyList_hp}{Lazy\+List} provides exclusive access to inserted item and does not require any node-\/level synchronization. 
\end{DoxyWarning}

\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Michael\+Hash\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Ordered\+List, Traits $>$\+::insert (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_a5d3f41494e647ab88a7301dae2cec6a0}{value\+\_\+type}} \&}]{val}{, }\item[{Func}]{f}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Inserts new node 

This function is intended for derived non-\/intrusive containers.

The function allows to split creating of new item into two part\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item create item with key only
\item insert new item into the set
\item if inserting is success, calls {\ttfamily f} functor to initialize value-\/field of {\ttfamily val}.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The functor signature is\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{benchmarks_2async__task_2async__task_8hpp_abce53bb5cc1ee70cdc013fd9b93547eb}{func}}(\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_a5d3f41494e647ab88a7301dae2cec6a0}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set}{val}}\ );}

\end{DoxyCode}
 where {\ttfamily val} is the item inserted. The user-\/defined functor is called only if the inserting is success.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
For \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_MichaelList_rcu}{Michael\+List} as the bucket see \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1intrusive_cds_intrusive_item_creating}{insert item troubleshooting}. \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_LazyList_rcu}{Lazy\+List} provides exclusive access to inserted item and does not require any node-\/level synchronization. 
\end{DoxyWarning}

Unlinks the item {\ttfamily val} from the set 

The function searches the item {\ttfamily val} in the set and unlink it if it is found and is equal to {\ttfamily val}.

The function returns {\ttfamily true} if success and {\ttfamily false} otherwise. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_a006ac3c03bb3891fb69fd278cbc30b82}\index{cds::intrusive::MichaelHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, OrderedList, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::MichaelHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, OrderedList, Traits $>$}!unlink@{unlink}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_a0aec8c9a65170566abba4b804d461348} 
std\+::pair$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} $>$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Michael\+Hash\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Ordered\+List, Traits $>$\+::update (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_a5d3f41494e647ab88a7301dae2cec6a0}{value\+\_\+type}} \&}]{val}{, }\item[{Func}]{func}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}}}]{b\+Allow\+Insert}{ = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a41f9c5fb8b08eb5dc3edce4dcb37fee7}{true}}}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Updates the element 

The operation performs inserting or changing data with lock-\/free manner.

If the item {\ttfamily val} not found in the set, then {\ttfamily val} is inserted iff {\ttfamily b\+Allow\+Insert} is {\ttfamily true}. Otherwise, the functor {\ttfamily func} is called with item found.

The functor signature depends of the type of {\ttfamily Ordered\+List\+:} 

{\bfseries{for {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{Michael\+List}}, {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{Lazy\+List}}}} 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set}{functor}}\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set}{operator()}}(\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set}{bNew}},\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set}{item}},\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set}{val}}\ );}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}
 with arguments\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily b\+New} -\/ {\ttfamily true} if the item has been inserted, {\ttfamily false} otherwise
\item {\ttfamily item} -\/ item of the set
\item {\ttfamily val} -\/ argument {\ttfamily val} passed into the {\ttfamily update}() function If new item has been inserted (i.\+e. {\ttfamily b\+New} is {\ttfamily true}) then {\ttfamily item} and {\ttfamily val} arguments refers to the same thing.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The functor may change non-\/key fields of the {\ttfamily item}. \begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
For \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_cds_intrusive_MichaelList_hp}{Michael\+List} as the bucket see \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1intrusive_cds_intrusive_item_creating}{insert item troubleshooting}. \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_cds_intrusive_LazyList_hp}{Lazy\+List} provides exclusive access to inserted item and does not require any node-\/level synchronization.
\end{DoxyWarning}
{\bfseries{for {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_iterable_list}{Iterable\+List}}}} 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{benchmarks_2async__task_2async__task_8hpp_abce53bb5cc1ee70cdc013fd9b93547eb}{func}}(\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_a5d3f41494e647ab88a7301dae2cec6a0}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set}{val}},\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_a5d3f41494e647ab88a7301dae2cec6a0}{value\_type}}\ *\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set}{old}}\ );}

\end{DoxyCode}
 where
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily val} -\/ argument {\ttfamily val} passed into the {\ttfamily update}() function
\item {\ttfamily old} -\/ old value that will be retired. If new item has been inserted then {\ttfamily old} is {\ttfamily nullptr}.
\end{DoxyItemize}

Returns {\ttfamily  std\+::pair$<$bool, bool$>$ } where {\ttfamily first} is {\ttfamily true} if operation is successful, {\ttfamily second} is {\ttfamily true} if new item has been added or {\ttfamily false} if the item with {\ttfamily key} already is in the set. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_a94048627cc5ce90ba4607d43ef1a1f0f}\index{cds::intrusive::MichaelHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, OrderedList, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::MichaelHashSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, OrderedList, Traits $>$}!update@{update}}

std\+::pair$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} $>$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Michael\+Hash\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Ordered\+List, Traits $>$\+::update (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_a5d3f41494e647ab88a7301dae2cec6a0}{value\+\_\+type}} \&}]{val}{, }\item[{Func}]{func}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}}}]{b\+Allow\+Insert}{ = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a41f9c5fb8b08eb5dc3edce4dcb37fee7}{true}}}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Updates the element 

The operation performs inserting or changing data with lock-\/free manner.

If the item {\ttfamily val} not found in the set, then {\ttfamily val} is inserted iff {\ttfamily b\+Allow\+Insert} is {\ttfamily true}. Otherwise, the functor {\ttfamily func} is called with item found. The functor signature is\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}

\end{DoxyCode}
 with arguments\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}

\item {\ttfamily item} -\/ item of the set
\item {\ttfamily val} -\/ argument {\ttfamily val} passed into the {\ttfamily update}() function If new item has been inserted (i.\+e. {\ttfamily b\+New} is {\ttfamily true}) then {\ttfamily item} and {\ttfamily val} arguments refers to the same thing.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The functor may change non-\/key fields of the {\ttfamily item}.

Returns {\ttfamily  std\+::pair$<$bool, bool$>$ } where {\ttfamily first} is {\ttfamily true} if operation is successful, {\ttfamily second} is {\ttfamily true} if new item has been added or {\ttfamily false} if the item with {\ttfamily key} already is in the set.

For \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_cds_intrusive_MichaelList_hp}{Michael\+List} as the bucket see \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1intrusive_cds_intrusive_item_creating}{insert item troubleshooting}. \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_cds_intrusive_LazyList_hp}{Lazy\+List} provides exclusive access to inserted item and does not require any node-\/level synchronization.

std\+::enable\+\_\+if$<$ std\+::is\+\_\+same$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_a5d3f41494e647ab88a7301dae2cec6a0}{value\+\_\+type}} $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__impl__opengl3__loader_8h_abe8e049f756b5ba547bda825af81b645}{\+::value}} \&\&is\+\_\+iterable\+\_\+list$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_ordered_list_00_01_traits_01_4_a2c7586c2c778c2fd5562adbd21fde73b}{ordered\+\_\+list}} $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__impl__opengl3__loader_8h_abe8e049f756b5ba547bda825af81b645}{\+::value}}, std\+::pair$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} $>$ $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__impl__opengl3__loader_8h_ae8396ff85d63082521e3324820df1009}{\+::type}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_hash_set}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Michael\+Hash\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Ordered\+List, Traits $>$\+::upsert (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} \&}]{val}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}}}]{b\+Allow\+Insert}{ = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a41f9c5fb8b08eb5dc3edce4dcb37fee7}{true}}}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Inserts or updates the node (only for {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_iterable_list}{Iterable\+List}}) 

The operation performs inserting or changing data with lock-\/free manner.

If the item {\ttfamily val} is not found in the set, then {\ttfamily val} is inserted iff {\ttfamily b\+Allow\+Insert} is {\ttfamily true}. Otherwise, the current element is changed to {\ttfamily val}, the old element will be retired later by call {\ttfamily Traits\+::disposer}.

Returns std\+::pair$<$bool, bool$>$ where {\ttfamily first} is {\ttfamily true} if operation is successful, {\ttfamily second} is {\ttfamily true} if {\ttfamily val} has been added or {\ttfamily false} if the item with that key already in the set.
